                                        id="{{ $val }}" data-id="{{ $val }}"

                                        <div class="card-body p-3" style="cursor: pointer;">
                                            <div class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between">
                                                <div class="d-flex align-items-center">
                                                    <div class="theme-avtar bg-primary">

                                                        <img src="{{ asset('Modules/VCard/Resources/assets/custom/icon/white/' . $val . '.svg') }}"

        var isSave = 0;
        $(function() {
            $(".sortable").sortable();
            $(".sortable").disableSelection();
            $(".sortable").sortable({
                stop: function() {
                    var order = [];
                    $(this).find('li').each(function(index, data) {
                        order[index] = $(data).attr('data-id');
                    });
                    $('#hidden_order').val(order);

                }
            });
            var block_order = [];
            $(".sortable").find('li').each(function(index, data) {
                block_order[index] = $(data).attr('data-id');
            });
            $('#hidden_order').val(block_order);

            $(".timepicker").datetimepicker({
                //format: "LT",
                format: "hh:mm A",
                timeZone: "America/New_York",
                icons: {
                    up: "fa fa-chevron-up",
                    down: "fa fa-chevron-down"
                }
            }).on("dp.change",function(e){
                var date = e.date;
                var target = $(e.target).attr('name');
                var data_preview_id = $(e.target).attr('data-id');

                var start_time_preview = $(`#${data_preview_id}_start`).val();
                var end_time_preview = $(`#${data_preview_id}_end`).val();
                var time_preview = start_time_preview + '-' + end_time_preview;
                if ($(`#${data_preview_id}`).prop('checked')) {
                    $(`.${data_preview_id}`).text(time_preview);
                    isSave = 1;
                    //console.log('Business isSave==>'+isSave);
                }
            });

            $(".appointmentTimepicker").datetimepicker({
                // format: "LT",
                format: "hh:mm A",
                timeZone: "America/New_York",
                icons: {
                    up: "fa fa-chevron-up",
                    down: "fa fa-chevron-down"
                }
            }).on("dp.change",function(e){
                var date = e.date;
                var target = $(e.target).attr('name');
                var el = $(e.target).attr('id');

                var appointmentTime = date.format("hh:mm A");
                $(`#${el}_preview`).text(appointmentTime);
                isSave = 1;
                //console.log('Appointment isSave==>'+isSave);
            });
        });

        function changeFunction(el) {
            var data_preview_id = $(`#${el}`).data('id');
            var start_time_preview = $(`#${data_preview_id}_start`).val();
            var end_time_preview = $(`#${data_preview_id}_end`).val();
            var time_preview = start_time_preview + '-' + end_time_preview;
            if ($(`#${data_preview_id}`).prop('checked')) {
                $(`.${data_preview_id}`).text(time_preview);
            }
        }

        function getRadio(el) {
            var get_val = $(el).val();
            var get_class = $(el).attr('class');
            $('.' + get_class).text(get_val);
            var span_star = '';
            const arr = [
                1,
                2,
                3,
                4,
                5
            ];
            $('#' + get_class + '_star').text('')
            $.each(arr, function(index, value) {

                if (value <= get_val) {
                    span_star = `<i class="star-color  fas fa-star"></i>`;
                } else {
                    span_star = `<i class="fa fa-star"></i>`;
                }
                $('#' + get_class + '_star').append(span_star);
            });
        }

        function validURL(str) {
            var pattern = new RegExp('^(https?:\\/\\/)?' + // protocol
                '((([a-z\\d]([a-z\\d-]*[a-z\\d])*)\\.)+[a-z]{2,}|' + // domain name
                '((\\d{1,3}\\.){3}\\d{1,3}))' + // OR ip (v4) address
                '(\\:\\d+)?(\\/[-a-z\\d%_@.~+]*)*' + // port and path
                '(\\?[;&a-z\\d%_.~+=-]*)?' + // query string
                '(\\#[-a-z\\d_]*)?$', 'i'); // fragment locator
            return !!pattern.test(str);
        }

        $("input").keyup(function() {
            var id = $(this).attr('id');
            var preview = $(`#${id}`).val();
            var section = $(`#${id}`).attr('data-section');
            if(preview == ''){
                if ($(this).attr('data-dTitle') !== undefined) {
                    preview = $(`#${id}`).attr('data-dTitle');
                    $(`#${id}`).val(preview);
                }else{
                    $(`#${section}, .section-title`).remove();
                }
            }
            console.log('id==>'+id);
            console.log('preview==>'+preview);
            $(`#${id}_preview`).text(preview);
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('Input For All Section isSave==>'+isSave);
        });

        $(".social_href").keyup(function() {
            var id = $(this).attr('id');
            var text = $(this).attr('name');
            var subtext = "Whatsapp";
            var isIncluded = text.includes(subtext);
            var preview = $(`#${id}`).val();
            var h_preview = validURL(preview);

            if (h_preview == true) {
                $(`#${id}_error_href`).text("");
                $(`#${id}_href_preview`).attr("href", preview);
            } else {
                if(isIncluded==false)
                {
                    $(`#${id}_error_href`).text("Please enter valid link");
                    $(`#${id}_href_preview`).attr("href", "#");
                }
            }
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('Social Link isSave==>'+isSave);
        });

        $("textarea").keyup(function() {
            var id = $(this).attr('id');
            //console.log(id);
            var preview = $(`#${id}`).val();
            $(`#${id}_preview`).text(preview);
            $(`.description-div`).show();
            if ($('.description-text').val() == "") {
                $(`.description-div`).hide();
            }
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('TextArea For All Section isSave==>'+isSave);
        });

        $(".days").change(function() {
            var day_id = $(this).attr('id');
            if ($(this).prop('checked')) {
                var this_attr_id = $(this).attr('id');
                var start_time = $(`#${this_attr_id}_start`).val();
                var end_time = $(`#${this_attr_id}_end`).val();
                if (start_time == '' && end_time == '') {
                    $(`.${day_id}`).text('00:00');

                } else {
                    var time = start_time + '-' + end_time;
                    $(`.${day_id}`).text(time);
                }
            } else {
                $(`.${day_id}`).text('Closed');
            }
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('Business Days For All Section isSave==>'+isSave);
        });

        function changeTime(el) {
            var time_input = $(`#${el}`).val();
            $(`#${el}_preview`).text(time_input);
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('Appointment Time For All Section isSave==>'+isSave);
        }

            }, 200);
            $(".theme-view-card").removeClass('selected-theme')
            $(this).closest('.theme-view-card').addClass('selected-theme');
        });

    <script>
        $(document).ready(function() {

        function setDefaultColor(){
            $('.colorPicker').each(function() {
                var sectionName = $(this).attr('data-name');
                var section = $(this).attr('data-section');
                var pickerType = $(this).attr('data-type');
                var personalInfo = ['title','designation','sub_title','description'];
                var fontId = $(this).attr('id');

                if ($.inArray(sectionName, personalInfo) == -1) {
                    var bgColorVal = $('#hidden_'+sectionName+'_color').val();
                    var fontColorVal = $('#hidden_'+sectionName+'_font_color').val();

                    var sliderButtons = $('#'+sectionName+'-div').find('.slick-prev, .slick-next');
                    sliderButtons.css('background-color', fontColorVal);

                    if(pickerType == 'bgColor' && bgColorVal == ""){
                        var bgColor = $('#'+section).css('background-color');
                        if (bgColor !== 'transparent' && bgColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                            var hexbgColor = rgbToHex(bgColor);
                        } else {
                            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme20']))
                                var defaultColor = $('.home-wrapper').css('background-color');
                            @else
                                var defaultColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background-color');
                            @endif
                            var hexbgColor = rgbToHex(defaultColor);
                        }
                        $(this).val(hexbgColor);
                    }

                    if(pickerType == 'fontColor' && fontColorVal == ""){
                        if(section == 'services-div'){
                            var fontColor = $('#services-div .service-card-inner').css('color');
                            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16']))
                                var fontColor = $('#services-div .service-card-inner p').css('color');
                            @endif
                        }else{
                            var fontColor = $('#'+section).css('color');
                            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16']))
                                if(section == 'business-hours-div'){
                                    var fontColor = $('#business-hours-div ul li').css('color');
                                }
                            @endif
                            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme5']))
                                if(section == 'contact-div'){
                                    var fontColor = $('#contact-div ul li a span').css('color');
                                }
                            @endif
                        }

                        if (fontColor !== 'transparent' && fontColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                            var hexfontColor = rgbToHex(fontColor);
                        } else {
                            var defaultFontColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('color');
                            var hexfontColor = rgbToHex(defaultFontColor);
                        }
                        $('#'+fontId).val(hexfontColor);
                    }
                }
            });

            var titleId = '{{$business->id}}_title_preview';
            var designationId = '{{$business->id}}_designation_preview';
            var subtitleId = '{{$business->id}}_subtitle_preview';
            var descriptionId = '{{$business->id}}_desc_preview';

            const divArray = ['title', 'designation', 'sub_title', 'description'];

                var fontColorVal = $('#hidden_'+divArray[index]+'_font_color').val();

                    var fontColor = $('#'+item).css('color');
                    if (fontColor !== 'transparent' && fontColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                        var hexfontColor = rgbToHex(fontColor);
                    } else {
                        var defaultFontColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('color');
                        var hexfontColor = rgbToHex(defaultFontColor);
                    }
                    $('#'+divArray[index]+'_font_color-picker').val(hexfontColor);
                }
            });

            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme1','theme2','theme5','theme6','theme7','theme16','theme20']))
                @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme5','theme6','theme7','theme20']))
                    var existBgColor = $('#hidden_first_color').val();
                    if(existBgColor == ""){
                        @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme5')
                            var profileSectionBgColor = $('.profile-section').css('background-color');
                        @elseif($card_theme->theme == 'theme20')
                            var profileSectionBgColor = $('.home-wrapper').css('background-color');
                        @else
                            var profileSectionBgColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background-color');
                        @endif
                        if (profileSectionBgColor !== 'transparent' && profileSectionBgColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                            @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme6')
                                var hexProfileColor = rgbToHex('rgb(172, 216, 254)');
                            @else
                                var hexProfileColor = rgbToHex(profileSectionBgColor);
                            @endif
                        } else {
                            var defaultBtnColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background-color');
                            var hexProfileColor = rgbToHex(defaultBtnColor);
                        }
                        $('#first_color-picker').val(hexProfileColor);
                    }
                @else
                    var existBgColor1 = $('#hidden_first_color1').val();
                    var existBgColor2 = $('#hidden_first_color2').val();
                    if(existBgColor1 == "" && existBgColor2 == ""){
                        @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme2')
                            var hexProfileColor1 = '#1840DA';
                            var hexProfileColor2 = '#E3E8F1';
                        @else
                            var profileSectionBgColor = $('.profile-section').css('background-image');
                            if (profileSectionBgColor !== 'transparent' && profileSectionBgColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                                var rgbValues = profileSectionBgColor.match(/rgb\((\d+), (\d+), (\d+)\)/g);
                                var hexProfileColor1 = rgbToHex(rgbValues[0]);
                                var hexProfileColor2 = rgbToHex(rgbValues[1]);

                                @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16']))
                                    var hexSocialColor = rgbToHex(rgbValues[1]);
                                    $('#social_color-pickervar').val(hexSocialColor);
                                @endif
                            } else {
                                var defaultProfileColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background-color');
                                var hexProfileColor1 = rgbToHex(defaultProfileColor);
                                var hexProfileColor2 = rgbToHex(defaultProfileColor);

                                @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16']))
                                $('#social_color-pickervar').val(hexProfileColor);
                                @endif
                            }
                        @endif

                        $('#first_color-picker1').val(hexProfileColor1);
                        $('#first_color-picker2').val(hexProfileColor2);
                    }
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme16')
                        var existTempBgColor = $('#hidden_template_color').val();
                        if(existTempBgColor == ""){
                            $('#template_color-picker').val('#ffffff');
                        }
                    @endif
                @endif
            @endif

            if (socialBorderColor !== 'transparent' && socialBorderColor !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {

        function rgbToHex(rgb) {
            if(rgb != undefined){
                // Convert the RGB string to an array of numbers
                var nums = rgb.match(/\d+/g);
                // Convert each number to hexadecimal and concatenate
                return "#" + nums.map(function(num) {
                    // Convert each number to hexadecimal and ensure it has two digits
                    return ('0' + parseInt(num).toString(16)).slice(-2);
                }).join('');
            }else{
                return '';
            }
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {

        $(document).on('change', '#is_custom_html_enabled', function(e) {
            $('.custom_html_text').hide();
            if ($("#is_custom_html_enabled").prop('checked') == true) {
                $('.custom_html_text').show();

            }else{
                $('.custom_html_text').hide();
                $('#custom_htmlColorPicker').hide();

        $(".input-text-location").each(function() {
            var textarea = $(this);
            var text = textarea.text();
            var div = $('<div id="temp"></div>');
            div.css({
                "width": "530px"
            });
            div.text(text);
            $('body').append(div);
            var divHeight = $('#temp').height();
            div.remove();
            divHeight += 32;
            this.setAttribute("style", "height:" + divHeight + "px;overflow-y:hidden;");
        }).on("input", function() {
            this.style.height = "auto";
            this.style.height = (this.scrollHeight) + "px";
        });
    </script>

        $('#download-qr').on('click', function() {
            var qrcode = '{{ $business->slug }}';
            $.ajax({
                url: '{{ route('download.qr') }}',
                type: 'GET',
                data: {
                    "qrData": qrcode,
                },
                success: function(data) {

                    if (data.success == true) {

                        $('#qrdata').html(data.data);
                    }
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        var element = document.querySelector("#qrdata");
                         saveCapture(element)

                        $("#qrcodeModal").removeClass("show");
                        $("#qrcodeModal").modal('hide');
                        $("body").css("overflow",'');
                       $("body").css("padding-right",'');
                        $('body').removeClass('modal-open');
                        $('#qrcodeModal').removeClass('modal-backdrop');
                        $(".modal-backdrop").removeClass("show");

                        $("#qrdata").html('');


                    }, 200);
                }
            });


        });

        $('.download_my_qr_code').on('click', function(e) {
            var enable_qr_code='on';
            var qrfilename='{{$business->title}}'+'.png';
            if(enable_qr_code=="on")
            {
                e.preventDefault();
                var img = new Image();
                img.src = $('.code').find('img').attr('src');
                img.onload = function() {
                    var canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    canvas.width = img.width;
                    canvas.height = img.height;
                    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
                    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                    var data = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
                    var a = document.createElement("a");
                    a.download = qrfilename;
                    a.href = data;
                    a.click();
                };
            }
            else
            {
                e.preventDefault();
                var img = new Image();
                img.src = $('.downloadqrcode').find('img').attr('src');
                img.onload = function() {
                    var canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    canvas.width = img.width;
                    canvas.height = img.height;
                    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
                    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                    var data = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
                    var a = document.createElement("a");
                    a.download = qrfilename;
                    a.href = data;
                    a.click();
                };
            }


        });

        $('.remove_gallery').on('click', function(e) {
            var this_id = $(this).data('id');
            var business_id = '{{$business->id}}';

                type: 'POST',

                },

                    $(this).closest('#inputFormRow5').remove();
                    $('.galleryData_'+this_id).remove();
                    var gId = $('#gallery_'+this_id).attr('data-slick-index');
                    $('.gallery-slider').slick('slickRemove', gId);

                    if ($('.gallery-slider').find('.slick-slide').length === 1 && $('.gallary_data').length === 0) {
                        console.log('in last slide');
                        $('.gallery-slider .slick-slide').last().remove();
                    }

                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var fColor = $('#hidden_gallery_font_color').val();
                        if(fColor != ""){
                            var btnStyle = $('#gallery-div').find('.slick-prev, .slick-next');
                            btnStyle.css('background-color', fColor);
                        }
                    }, 100);
                }
            });

        function download(url) {
            var a = $("<a style='display:none' id='js-downloder'>")
                .attr("href", url)
                .attr("download", "{{ $business->slug }}")
                .appendTo("body");
            a[0].click();
            a.remove();
        }

        function saveCapture(element) {
            html2canvas(element).then(function(canvas) {
                download(canvas.toDataURL("image/png"));
            })
        }

        function canvasdata() {
            html2canvas($('#qrdata'), {
                onrendered: function(canvas) {
                    var a = document.createElement('a');
                    // toDataURL defaults to png, so we need to request a jpeg, then convert for file download.
                    a.href = canvas.toDataURL("image/jpeg").replace("image/jpeg", "image/octet-stream");
                    a.download = 'somefilename.jpg';
                    a.click();
                }
            });
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('.theme-slider').slick('refresh');
        });

        $(document).ready(function() {
            var slug = '{{ $business->slug }}';
            var url_link = `{{ url('/cards') }}/${slug}`;
            $(`.qr-link`).text(url_link);
            $('.qrcode').qrcode(url_link);

            let ele = $(".emojiarea").emojioneArea();
            $.each( ele, function( key, value ) {
                ele[key].emojioneArea.on("emojibtn.click keyup", function(btn, event) {
                    var get_id = ele[key].getAttribute('id');
                    var get_val = btn.html();
                    get_val = get_val.replace('&nbsp','');

                    var newVal = $('#'+get_id).data("emojioneArea").getText();
                    $(`#${get_id}_preview`).text(newVal);
                    $(`.description-div`).show();
                    if ($('.description-text').val() == "") {
                        $(`.description-div`).hide();
                    }
                    isSave = 1;
                    //console.log('isSave in Emoji==>'+isSave);
                });
            });
        });

        //Gallery
        function getSelectedGalleryValue(){
            var checked = $("input[type=radio][name='galleryoption']:checked");
            var id = $(checked).attr("id");
            if(id=='enable_video')
            {
                $('.video').show();
                $('.image').hide();
                $('.custom_image').hide();
                $('.custom_video').hide();
                $('.video').addClass('d-block');
                $('.video').removeClass('d-none');
                $('.image').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_image').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_video').addClass('d-none');
            }
            else if(id=='enable_image'){
                $('.image').show();
                $('.video').hide();
                $('.custom_image').hide();
                $('.custom_video').hide();
                $('.image').addClass('d-block');
                $('.image').removeClass('d-none');
                $('.video').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_image').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_video').addClass('d-none');
            }else if(id=='enable_custom_image_link'){
                $('.video').hide();
                $('.image').hide();
                $('.custom_image').show();
                $('.custom_video').hide();
                $('.custom_image').addClass('d-block');
                $('.custom_image').removeClass('d-none');
                $('.image').addClass('d-none');
                $('.video').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_video').addClass('d-none');
            }
            else if(id=='enable_custom_video_link'){
                $('.video').hide();
                $('.image').hide();
                $('.custom_image').hide();
                $('.custom_video').show();
                $('.custom_video').addClass('d-block');
                $('.custom_video').removeClass('d-none');
                $('.image').addClass('d-none');
                $('.video').addClass('d-none');
                $('.custom_image').addClass('d-none');
            }
        }

        function getSelectedSocialValue(id, no){
            console.log('Social==>'+no);
            if(id==`enable_video_${no}`)
            {
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).show();
                $(`.simage_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).addClass('d-block');
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).removeClass('d-none');
                $(`.simage_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
            }
            else if(id==`enable_image_${no}`){
                $(`.simage_${no}`).show();
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.simage_${no}`).addClass('d-block');
                $(`.simage_${no}`).removeClass('d-none');
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
            }else if(id==`enable_custom_image_link_${no}`){
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.simage_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).show();
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).addClass('d-block');
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).removeClass('d-none');
                $(`.simage_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
            }
            else if(id==`enable_custom_video_link_${no}`){
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.simage_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).hide();
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).show();
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).addClass('d-block');
                $(`.scustom_video_${no}`).removeClass('d-none');
                $(`.simage_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.svideo_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
                $(`.scustom_image_${no}`).addClass('d-none');
            }
        }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $('.cp_link').on('click', function() {
            var value = $(this).attr('data-link');
            var $temp = $("<input>");
            $("body").append($temp);
            $temp.val(value).select();
            document.execCommand("copy");
            $temp.remove();
            toastrs('{{ __('Success') }}', '{{ __('Link Copy on Clipboard') }}', 'success');
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function enablecookie() {
            const element = $('#enable_cookie').is(':checked');
            $('.cookieDiv').addClass('disabledCookie');
            if (element==true) {
                $('.cookieDiv').removeClass('disabledCookie');
                $("#cookie_logging").attr('checked', true);
                $('.ai_cookie').removeClass('disabledCookie');
            } else {
                $('.cookieDiv').addClass('disabledCookie');
                $("#cookie_logging").attr('checked', false);
                $('.ai_cookie').addClass('disabledCookie');
            }
        }

        //Custom Qr Code Scripts
        $('.qr_type').on('click', function () {
            $("input[type=radio][name='qr_type']").attr('checked', false);
            $("input[type=radio][name='qr_type']").parent().removeClass('btn-primary');
            $("input[type=radio][name='qr_type']").parent().addClass('btn-secondary');

            var value=$(this).children().attr('checked', true);
            var qr_type_val=$(this).children().attr('id');

            if(qr_type_val == 0){
                $('#qr_type_option').slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
            }else if(qr_type_val == 2){
                $('#qr_type_option').slideDown();
                $('#text_div').slideDown();
                $('#image_div').slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
            } else if(qr_type_val == 4){
                $('#qr_type_option').slideDown();
                $('#text_div').slideUp();
                $('#image_div').slideDown();
                $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
            }
            generate_qr();
        });

        function generate_qr() {
            if($("input[name='qr_type']:checked").parent().hasClass('btn-primary')==false)
            {
                var chekced=$("input[name='qr_type']:checked").parent().addClass('btn-primary');
                var qr_type_val=$("input[name='qr_type']:checked").attr('id');
                if(qr_type_val == 0){
                    $('#qr_type_option').slideUp();
                    $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                    $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
                }else if(qr_type_val == 2){
                    $('#qr_type_option').slideDown();
                    $('#text_div').slideDown();
                    $('#image_div').slideUp();
                    $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                    $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
                } else if(qr_type_val == 4){
                    $('#qr_type_option').slideDown();
                    $('#text_div').slideUp();
                    $('#image_div').slideDown();
                    $(this).removeClass('btn-secondary');
                    $(this).addClass('btn-primary');
                }

            }
            var card_url = '{{ env('APP_URL').''.$business->slug }}';

            $('.code').empty().qrcode({
                render: 'image',
                size: 500,
                ecLevel: 'H',
                minVersion: 3,
                quiet: 1,
                text: card_url,
                fill: $('.foreground_color').val(),
                background: $('.background_color').val(),
                radius: .01 * parseInt($('.radius').val(), 10),
                mode: parseInt($("input[name='qr_type']:checked").val(), 10),
                label: $('.qr_text').val(),
                fontcolor: $('.qr_text_color').val(),
                image: $("#image-buffer")[0],
                mSize: .01 * parseInt($('.qr_size').val(), 10)
            });
        }

        $('.qr_data').on('change', function () {
            generate_qr();
        });

         $('.qr_keyup').on('keyup', function () {
             generate_qr();
         });

        $(document).on('change', '.qr_image', function(e) {
            var img_reader, img_input = $('.qr_image')[0];
            img_input.files && img_input.files[0] && ((img_reader = new window.FileReader).onload = function (event) {
                $("#image-buffer").attr("src", event.target.result);
                setTimeout(generate_qr, 250)
            }, img_reader.readAsDataURL(img_input.files[0]))
        });
        generate_qr();

          $('.uploaded_image_name').text(uploaded_image_name.files.item(0).name);
        }

    <script>
        function submitForm(e) {
            var banner_val = '{{$business->banner}}';
            var logo_val = '{{$business->logo}}';

            var returnMethod1 = 0;
            var returnMethod2 = 0;

            @if(!in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme1','theme5','theme16','theme20']))
                var banner = $('input[name=banner]')[0].files[0];
                var banner_method = $('#banner_method').val();
            @else
                returnMethod1 = 1;
            @endif

            @if(!in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme20']))
                var logo = $('input[name=logo]')[0].files[0];
                var logo_method = $('#logo_method').val();
            @else
                returnMethod2 = 1;
            @endif

            if(banner_val==null || banner_val=='' || logo_val==null ||logo_val==''){
                if(returnMethod1 == 0){
                    if(banner_method == 0 && (banner==undefined || banner=='')){
                        $(`#banner_validate`).text("Banner Field is required");
                        alert("Banner Field is required");
                        return false;
                    }
                } else if(returnMethod2 == 0){
                    if(logo_method == 0 && (logo==undefined || logo=='')){
                        $(`#banner_validate`).text("Logo Field is required");
                        alert("Logo Field is required");
                        return false;
                    }
                } else{
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }

        function checkImageSize(imageSize, iType){
            var maxSizeInBytes = $('#fileUploadSize').val();
            if(imageSize > maxSizeInBytes){
                $(`#banner_validate`).empty();
                $(`#banner_validate`).html("The "+iType+" may not be greater than 5MB.");
                alert('The '+iType+' may not be greater than 5MB.');
                return 0;
            }else{
                return 1;
            }
        }

        function findRequiredFieldsInAccordion() {
            let allRequiredFieldsFilled = true;
            const accordionItems = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-item');
            accordionItems.forEach(item => {
                const accordionButton = item.querySelector('.accordion-button');
                const accordionBody = item.querySelector('.accordion-body');
                const requiredFields = item.querySelectorAll('.accordion-body input[required]');

                for (let i = 0; i < requiredFields.length; i++) {
                    if (requiredFields[i].value.trim() === '') {
                        const validationMessage = document.createElement('div');
                        $('.validation-message').remove();
                        validationMessage.className = 'validation-message text-danger';
                        validationMessage.textContent = 'This field is required';
                        requiredFields[i].insertAdjacentElement('afterend', validationMessage);

                        if (accordionButton.classList.contains('collapsed')) {
                            accordionButton.click();
                        }

                        //accordionButton.click();

                        requiredFields[i].focus();
                        allRequiredFieldsFilled = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            });

            if (allRequiredFieldsFilled) {
                $('#editBusinessForm').submit();
            }
        }

        function changeValue(el) {
        // Get a reference to the select element
            var selectElement = document.getElementById(el);
            // Check if the element exists before attaching the event listener
            var selectedOption = selectElement.options[selectElement.selectedIndex];
            var selectedName = selectedOption.value;
            document.getElementById(el + '_preview').textContent = selectedName;
        }

        $('.colorPicker').on('change', function(){
            var cType = $(this).attr('data-type');
            var sectionDiv = $(this).attr('data-section');
            var sectionName = $(this).attr('data-name');
            var color = $(this).val();

            if(cType == 'bgColor'){
                $('#hidden_'+sectionName+'_color').val(color);

                @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme1','theme2','theme16']))
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme2')
                        var color1 = $('#first_color-picker1').val();
                        var color2 = $('#first_color-picker2').val();
                        changeBeforeBackground('#view_theme12 .profile-section .profile-cover', color1,2);
                        $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background', color2);
                    @endif

                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme16')
                        var tempColor = $('#template_color-picker').val();
                        console.log('on change ==>'+tempColor);
                        $('.home-wrapper').css('background', tempColor);
                    @endif

                    if(sectionDiv == 'first-div'){
                        var color1 = $('#first_color-picker1').val();
                        var color2 = $('#first_color-picker2').val();

                        @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme1')
                            var gradient = 'linear-gradient(to bottom, '+color1+' 65%, '+color2+' 56%)';
                            $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background', gradient);
                        @else
                            var gradient = 'linear-gradient(to bottom, '+color1+' 30%, '+color2+' 25% 100%)';
                            $('#'+sectionDiv).css('background', gradient);
                        @endif

                        $('#hidden_first_color1').val(color1);
                        $('#hidden_first_color2').val(color2);
                    }else{
                        if(sectionName == 'description'){
                            $('#description-div').css('background', color);
                        }else{
                            $('#'+sectionDiv).css('background', color);
                        }
                    }
                @else
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme7')
                        $('#'+sectionDiv).css('background', color);
                        $('.user-name').css('background', color);
                    @endif
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme8')
                        $('#'+sectionDiv).css('background', color);
                        $('.profile-section').css('background', color);
                    @endif
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme6')
                        if(sectionName == 'first'){
                            changeBeforeBackground('#view_theme16 .profile-section .profile-cover', color,6);
                        }
                    @endif
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme2')
                        if(sectionName == 'first'){
                            changeBeforeBackground('#view_theme12 .profile-section .profile-cover', color,2);
                        }
                    @endif
                    @if($card_theme->theme == 'theme14')
                        if(sectionName == 'first'){
                            console.log('theme 14 color==>'+color);
                            changeBeforeBackground('#view_theme3 .home-banner-section', color,14);
                        }
                    @endif
                    $('#'+sectionDiv).css('background', color);
                @endif

                if(sectionName == 'appointment'){
                    @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme16','theme20']))
                        $('#appointmentForm').css('background-color', color + ' !important');
                    @else
                        $('.appointment-modal .modal-dialog .modal-content').css('background-color', color + ' !important');
                        var mdArr = ['.modal-header','.modal-body','.modal-footer'];
                        $.each(mdArr, function(index, value){
                            var existStyle = $(".appointment-modal"+ " " + value).attr('style');
                            if(existStyle != undefined){
                                var newStyle = existStyle + " background:"+color+"!important;";
                            }else{
                                var newStyle = "background:"+color+"!important;";
                            }
                            $(".appointment-modal"+ " " + value).attr('style',newStyle);
                        });
                    @endif
                    $(".picker__day--highlighted, .picker__button--close").css('background-color', color);
                }

                if(sectionName == 'product'){
                    $("#"+sectionDiv+" button").css('background', color);
                }

                if(sectionName == 'social') {
                    $('.more-info').css('background', color);
                    @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme16','theme20']))
                        $('.share-card-wrapper').css('background', color);
                        $('#contactFormModal').css('background', color);
                    @else
                        $('.share-card .modal-dialog .modal-content').css('background-color', color+'!important');

                        var mdArr = ['.modal-body'];
                        $.each(mdArr, function(index, value){
                            var existStyle = $(".share-card"+ " " + value).attr('style');
                            var gradient = 'linear-gradient(to bottom, '+color+' 35%, var(--second-color) 35%)';
                            if(existStyle != undefined){
                                var newStyle = existStyle + " background-image:"+gradient+"!important;";
                            }else{
                                var newStyle = "background-image:"+gradient+"!important;";
                            }
                            $(".share-card"+ " " + value).attr('style',newStyle);
                        });
                        var cmdArr = ['.modal-header','.modal-body','.modal-footer'];
                        $.each(cmdArr, function(index, value){
                            var existStyle = $(".contact-modal"+ " " + value).attr('style');
                            if(existStyle != undefined){
                                var newStyle = existStyle + " background-color:"+color+"!important;";
                            }else{
                                var newStyle = "background-color:"+color+"!important;";
                            }
                            $(".contact-modal"+ " " + value).attr('style',newStyle);
                        });
                    @endif

                    var brandStyle = $('.nx-copyright').attr('style');
                    if(brandStyle != undefined){
                        var newBStyle = brandStyle + " background:"+color+"!important;";
                    }else{
                        var newBStyle = "background:"+color+"!important;";
                    }
                    $('.nx-copyright').attr('style',newBStyle);
                }
            }
            if(cType == 'fontColor'){
                if(sectionName == 'title' || sectionName == 'designation' || sectionName == 'sub_title' || sectionName == 'description'){
                    @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16','theme20']))
                        if(sectionName != 'description'){
                            $('#'+sectionDiv).removeAttr('class');
                        }
                    @else
                        $('#'+sectionDiv).removeAttr('class');
                    @endif
                    $('#'+sectionDiv).css('color', color+'!important');
                }

                if(sectionName == 'appointment'){
                    var cssProperties = {
                        'color': color,
                        'border-color': color,
                    };
                    $("#"+sectionDiv+" input[name='date']").css(cssProperties);
                    @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme16','theme20']))
                        $("#appointment-div .app_select").css(cssProperties);
                    @endif
                    $("#"+sectionDiv+" label").css(cssProperties);
                    var existBtnStyle = $("#"+sectionDiv+" button").attr('style');
                    if(existBtnStyle != undefined){
                        var newstyle = existBtnStyle +'; border-color:'+color+'; color:'+color
                    }else{
                        var newstyle = 'border-color:'+color+'; color:'+color
                    }
                    $("#"+sectionDiv+" button").attr('style', newstyle);

                        $(".appointment-modal"+ " " + value).find('*').each(function() {
                            var existStyle = $(this).attr('style');
                            if(existStyle != undefined){
                                var newStyle = existStyle + " border-color:"+color+"; color:"+color+"!important;";
                            }else{
                                var newStyle = "border-color:"+color+"; color:"+color+"!important;";
                            }
                            $(this).attr('style',newStyle);
                        });
                    });
                }

                if(sectionName == 'social'){
                    @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme16','theme20']))
                        var totalsBtn = $('#social-div .btn');

                        if (totalsBtn.length > 0) {
                            totalsBtn.each(function(index, element) {
                                var sbtnStyle = $(element).attr('style');

                                } else {
                                    var newBtnStyle = "color:" + color + "!important;";

                    @endif

                    $('.more-info h2').removeAttr('class');

                    $('.more-info a').css('color', color);

                    if(sectionName == 'social' && (curTheme == 'theme14' || curTheme == 'theme16' || curTheme == 'theme20')){
                        return;
                    }else{

                        if(existStyle != undefined){

                        }else{
                            var newStyle = "color:"+color+"!important;";

                        }

                btnStyle.css('background-color', color);
                $('#hidden_'+sectionName+'_font_color').val(color);
            }

        $('.theme-detail-body').on('click', '.close-btn', function (event) {
        //$('.close-btn').on('click', function(){
            var element = $(this).attr('data-id');
            if (element.length > 0) {
                var dsection = $(this).attr('data-section');
                if(dsection != "" || dsection != undefined){
                    if(dsection == "social"){
                        var ditem = $(this).attr('data-item');
                        if(dsection != "" || dsection != undefined){
                            $('#socialDiv_'+ditem).remove();
                        }
                    }
                }
                $('#'+element).remove();
            }

            if($(this).attr('id') == 'removeRow_testimonials'){
                $('.testimonial-slider').slick('refresh');
            }
        });

        function updateProductPurchaseLink(pId, link){
            if(link != ""){
                $('#product_link_title_'+pId+'_preview').attr('href',link)
            }else{
                $('#product_link_title_'+pId+'_preview').attr('href','javascript:void(0)')
            }
        }

        function updateServicesLink(sId, link){
            if(link != ""){
                $('#link_title_'+sId+'_preview').attr('href',link)
            }else{
                $('#link_title_'+sId+'_preview').attr('href','javascript:void(0)')
            }
        }

        function updateContactLink(cId, link, element){
            console.log('element==>'+element);
            if(link != ""){
                if (element == 'Phone'){
                    var nLink = 'tel:'+link;
                }else if(element == 'Email'){
                    var nLink = 'mailto:'+link;
                }else if (element == 'Whatsapp'){
                    var nLink = '{{url('https://wa.me/')}}'+link;
                }else{
                    var nLink = link;
                }
                $('#contact_link_'+cId+'_preview').attr('href',nLink);
            }else{
                $('#contact_link_'+cId+'_preview').attr('href','javascript:void(0)')
            }
            isSave = 1;
            //console.log('Contact Link isSave==>'+isSave);
        }

        $('.customSectionTitle').on('keyup', function(){
            var customTitle = $(this).val();
            var section = $(this).attr('data-section');
            if(customTitle != ""){
                $('#'+section+' h2').html(customTitle);
            }
        });

        /*Change Social Item Border Color*/
        $('.socialBorderColor').on('change', function(){
            var color = $(this).val();
            $('#social-div a').removeClass('socialBorder').css('border-color', color);
            $('#hidden_socials_border_color').val(color);
        });

        /*Change More Button Background Color*/
        $('.moreBtnColor').on('change', function(){
           var btnBgColor = $(this).val();
           $('.more-info a').css('background-color',btnBgColor);
           $('#hidden_more_btn_color').val(btnBgColor);
        });

        /*Change Appointment Button Color*/
        $('.appointmentButtonColor').on('change', function(){
            var color = $(this).val();

            @if(in_array($card_theme->theme,['theme14','theme16','theme20']))
                var elementStyle = 'section#appointment-div .btn';
            @else
                var elementStyle = '#appointment-div button';
            @endif
            var existingStyle = $(elementStyle).attr('style');
            var newStyle = existingStyle + "; background-color: " + color + " !important;";
            $(elementStyle).attr('style',newStyle);
            $('#hidden_appointment_button_color').val(color);

            var mdArr = ['.modal-header','.modal-body','.modal-footer'];
            $.each(mdArr, function(index, value){
                $(".appointment-modal"+ " " + value).find('button').each(function() {
                    var existStyle = $(this).attr('style');
                    if(existStyle != undefined){
                        var newStyle = existStyle + " background-color:"+color+"!important;";
                    }else{
                        var newStyle = "background-color:"+color+"!important;";
                    }
                    $(this).attr('style',newStyle);
                });
            });
        });

        /*Change Appointment Button Text*/
        $('#appointment_button_text').on('keyup', function(){
            if($(this).val() == ""){
                var btnText = 'Make An Appointment';
            }else{
                var btnText = $(this).val();
            }
            $('#appointment-div .appointment-modal-toggle').html(btnText);
        });

        /*Add Slide In Gallery Slider Just For Preview*/
        $('#custom_image_link_new').on('keyup', function(){
            var newImg = $(this).val();
            if($('.gallary_data').length === 0){
                $('.gallery-slider').slick('slickRemove', null, null, true);
            }
            $('.gallery-slider').slick('slickAdd', '<div class="gallery-itm newGalleryImage"><div class="gallery-media"><a href="javascript:;" id="imagepopup" tabindex="0" class="imagepopup"><img src="' + newImg + '" class="imageresource"></a></div></div>');
            setTimeout(function() {
                var fColor = $('#hidden_gallery_font_color').val();
                if(fColor != ""){
                    var btnStyle = $('#gallery-div').find('.slick-prev, .slick-next');
                    btnStyle.css('background-color', fColor);
                }
            }, 100);
        });

        /*Default Currency Set With Price*/
        function changePrice(price, proItem){
            var currency = $('#product_currency_select'+proItem).val();
            $('#product_currency_select'+proItem+'_preview').html(currency);
            $('#product_price_'+proItem+'_preview').html(price);
        }

        function timeSlots(element){
            var timeslots = document.getElementsByClassName('timeSlots');
            console.log(timeslots.length);
            for (var i = 0; i < timeslots.length; i++) {
                timeslots[i].style.removeProperty('background-color');
            }

            var appointment_btn_bg_color = $('section#appointment-div .btn').css('background-color');
            if (appointment_btn_bg_color !== 'transparent' && appointment_btn_bg_color !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {
                var hexappbtnColor = rgbToHex(appointment_btn_bg_color);
            } else {
                var defaultAppBtnColor = $('.bussiness-card-body').css('background-color');
                var hexappbtnColor = rgbToHex(defaultAppBtnColor);
            }

            @if(isset($appoinment->btn_color) && !empty($appoinment->btn_color))
            var btncolor = '{{$appoinment->btn_color}}';
            @else
            var btncolor = hexappbtnColor;
            @endif

            var existStyle = $(element).attr('style');
            if(existStyle != undefined){
                var nStyle = existStyle + 'background-color: '+btncolor;
            }else{
                var nStyle = 'background-color: '+btncolor;
            }
            $(element).attr('style',nStyle);
        }

        $('.timeSlots').on('click', function(){
            timeSlots($(this));
        });

        /*Focus On Specific Div On Template*/
        $('.accordion-header').on('click', function(){
            var targetDiv = $(this).data('id');
            $('#sticky #'+targetDiv).get(0).scrollIntoView();
        });

        /*For Simple Input*/
        $('#editBusinessForm :input').on('input', function() {
            isSave = 1;
            console.log('isSave in jQuery ==> ' + isSave);
        });

        /*Function For Auto Save Data Every 30 Sec*/
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $.ajaxSetup({
                headers: {
                    'X-CSRF-TOKEN': $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('content')
                }
            });
            function sendFormData() {
                console.log('auto save function running');
                //return false;
                $('#isAjax').val(1);
                var formData = new FormData($('#editBusinessForm')[0]);
                $.ajax({
                    url: '{{route('business.mUpdate',['business' => $business->id])}}',
                    method: 'POST',
                    data: formData,
                    processData: false,
                    contentType: false,
                    success: function(response) {
                        isSave = 0;
                        $('#isAjax').val(0);
                        // console.log('isSave==>'+isSave);
                        console.log('Data auto save successfully');
                        // alert('Form Save');
                    },
                    error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                        //console.error('Error sending data:', textStatus, errorThrown);
                    }
                });
            }
            // Call sendFormData every 30 seconds
            setInterval(function() {
                if (isSave == 1) {
                    sendFormData();
                }
            }, 30000);
        });

        function getBackgroundValue(selector, pseudoElement) {
            // Create a temporary element
            const tempElement = $('<div>').css({
                'background': window.getComputedStyle(
                    document.querySelector(selector), pseudoElement
                ).getPropertyValue('background')
            });

            // Append the temporary element to the body
            $('body').append(tempElement);

            // Extract the computed background value
            const backgroundValue = tempElement.css('background');

            // Remove the temporary element
            tempElement.remove();

            return backgroundValue;
        }

        function changeBeforeBackground(selector, color, theme) {
            var styleElement = $('#dynamic-before-style');

            // If the style element doesn't exist, create it
            if (styleElement.length === 0) {
                styleElement = $('<style id="dynamic-before-style"></style>').appendTo('head');
            }

            // Add or update the CSS rule for the ::before pseudo-element
            if(theme == 2){
                var newRule = selector + '::before { background: linear-gradient(180deg, '+color+' 34.23%, rgba(24, 64, 218, 0) 100%)!important;}';
            }
            if(theme == 6){
                var newRule = selector + '::before { background: linear-gradient(180deg, rgba(172, 216, 254, 0) 37.38%, ' + color + ' 61.71%)!important;}';
            }
            if(theme == 14){
                var newRule = selector + '::before { background: ' + color + '!important;}';
            }
            styleElement.text(newRule);
        }

        function removeItem(id){
            $('#'+id).remove();
        }
    </script>
@endpush
